<div class="mf-section-0" id="mf-section-0">
<p>Trong bài viết này, wikiHow sẽ hướng dẫn bạn cách sử dụng phần mềm Terminal trên Linux để tạo tệp văn bản. Sau khi tạo tệp, bạn có thể dùng phần mềm chỉnh sửa cài đặt sẵn trên Linux để chỉnh sửa văn bản. 
</p>

<div class="step_num">1</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Mở Terminal.</b> Để mở phần mềm, bạn hãy nhấp chuột vào <b>Menu</b> (Trình đơn) rồi tìm phần mềm Terminal, trông gần giống một tấm bảng đen có ký hiệu "&gt;_" màu trắng và nhấp chuột vào đó. Bạn thường tìm thấy Terminal ở thanh bên trái cửa sổ Menu.
<ul><li>Bạn có thể nhấp chuột vào thanh tìm kiếm ở ngay đầu cửa sổ Menu và nhập <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">terminal</kbd> để tìm Terminal.</li></ul>

<div class="step_num">2</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Nhập <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">ls</kbd> vào Terminal, sau đó nhấn <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;"><span class="Unicode">↵</span> Enter</kbd></b></span>.</b> Terminal sẽ mở danh mục chính nhưng lệnh <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">ls</kbd> sẽ hiện thị mọi thư mục trong danh mục hiện hành. Để tạo tệp văn bản ở một trong các danh mục đó, bạn cần thay đổi danh mục hiện hành.
</div>

<div class="step_num">3</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Tìm danh mục bạn muốn tạo tệp văn bản.</b> Bất kỳ tên danh mục nào được liệt kê phía dưới lệnh <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">ls</kbd> (ví dụ "Desktop") đều là địa điểm có thể điều hướng.
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-03">
<a name="step_1_4" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-4-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 4" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/75/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-4-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-4-Version-3.jpg" id="43ba1d6dfa30df70ff23f195c5015991" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/7/75/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-4-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-4-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('43ba1d6dfa30df70ff23f195c5015991')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 4" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/7/75/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-4-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-4-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/75/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-4-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-4-Version-3.jpg" id="43ba1d6dfa30df70ff23f195c5015991" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/7\/75\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-4-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-4-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/7\/75\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-4-Version-3.jpg\/v4-760px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-4-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":760,"bigHeight":570,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num">4</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Nhập  <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">cd directory</kbd>.</b> Bạn thay "directory" bằng tên danh mục muốn tạo tệp. Lệnh này sẽ chuyển sự tập trung của Terminal từ danh mục hiện hành sang danh mục mà bạn kể tên.
<ul>
<li>Ví dụ, bạn nhập lệnh <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">cd Desktop</kbd> để chuyển vị trí thực thi lệnh của Terminal sang danh mục Desktop.</li>
<li>Nếu muốn tạo tệp văn bản trong một thư mục riêng thuộc danh mục được chọn, bạn chỉ cần thêm dấu "/" sau tên danh mục rồi gõ tên thư mục. Ví dụ, với thư mục "Misc" trong danh mục Documents, bạn gõ <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">cd Documents/Misc</kbd>.</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-04">
<a name="step_1_5" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-5-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 5" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/a/a1/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-5-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-5-Version-3.jpg" id="ca8e3a82df0d2f8428c8beb6dce41456" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/a/a1/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-5-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-5-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('ca8e3a82df0d2f8428c8beb6dce41456')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 5" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/a/a1/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-5-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-5-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/a/a1/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-5-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-5-Version-3.jpg" id="ca8e3a82df0d2f8428c8beb6dce41456" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/a\/a1\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-5-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-5-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/a\/a1\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-5-Version-3.jpg\/v4-760px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-5-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":760,"bigHeight":570,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num">5</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Nhấn <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;"><span class="Unicode">↵</span> Enter</kbd></b></span>.</b> Đây là thao tác thực thi lệnh, chuyển mục tiêu của Terminal từ danh mục chính sang danh mục bạn chỉ định.
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-05">
<a name="step_1_6" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-6-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 6" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/6/65/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-6-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-6-Version-3.jpg" id="f3b9274b424fc32bc2db9946988c9baf" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/6/65/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-6-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-6-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('f3b9274b424fc32bc2db9946988c9baf')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 6" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/6/65/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-6-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-6-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/6/65/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-6-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-6-Version-3.jpg" id="f3b9274b424fc32bc2db9946988c9baf" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/6\/65\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-6-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-6-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/6\/65\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-6-Version-3.jpg\/v4-760px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-6-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":760,"bigHeight":570,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num">6</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Quyết định phần mềm chỉnh sửa.</b> Bạn có thể <a href="#-step_2_1">tạo tệp văn bản đơn giản</a> một cách nhanh chóng, hoặc sử dụng <a href="#step_3_1">Vim</a> hoặc <a href="#step_4_1">Emacs</a> để tạo và chỉnh sửa tệp nâng cao. Bạn đã truy cập vào danh mục muốn tạo tệp văn bản, giờ hãy tiến hành tạo tệp.
</div>

<div class="section steps  sticky"><div id="cácbước_2" class="section_text">
<h3 class="in-block">
<div class="altblock"><div>Phần <span>2</span><span class="method_of_count"> của 4:</span>
</div>
</div>
<span id="Tạo-Tệp-Văn-bản-Nhanh"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="T.E1.BA.A1o-T.E1.BB.87p-V.C4.83n-b.E1.BA.A3n-Nhanh">Tạo Tệp Văn bản Nhanh</span>
</h3>
<ol class="steps_list_2">
<li id="step-id-16">
<a name="step_2_1" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-7-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 7" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/b/be/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-7-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-7-Version-3.jpg" id="794781b147e78966373f8d6a6c75e304" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/b/be/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-7-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-7-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('794781b147e78966373f8d6a6c75e304')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 7" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/b/be/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-7-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-7-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/b/be/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-7-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-7-Version-3.jpg" id="794781b147e78966373f8d6a6c75e304" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/b\/be\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-7-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-7-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/b\/be\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-7-Version-3.jpg\/v4-760px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-7-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":760,"bigHeight":570,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num">1</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Nhập <b><code>cat &gt; tên tệp.txt</code> vào Terminal.</b></b> Bạn thay thế "tên tệp" bằng tên bạn muốn đặt cho tệp (ví dụ "báo cáo").
<ul><li>Ví dụ: khi tạo tệp "kitty", bạn nhập lệnh <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">cat &gt; kitty.txt</kbd>.</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-17">
<a name="step_2_2" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-8-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 8" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/8/8c/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-8-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-8-Version-3.jpg" id="e61e3081b14085df4903fb1728bc3c3d" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/8/8c/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-8-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-8-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('e61e3081b14085df4903fb1728bc3c3d')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 8" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/8/8c/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-8-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-8-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/8/8c/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-8-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-8-Version-3.jpg" id="e61e3081b14085df4903fb1728bc3c3d" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/8\/8c\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-8-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-8-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/8\/8c\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-8-Version-3.jpg\/v4-760px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-8-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":760,"bigHeight":570,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num">2</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Nhấn <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;"><span class="Unicode">↵</span> Enter</kbd></b></span>.</b> Đây là thao tác tạo tệp văn bản mới theo tên vừa đặt trong danh mục hiện hành. Con trỏ sẽ xuất hiện ở một dòng trống trong Terminal.
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-18">
<a name="step_2_3" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-9-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 9" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/77/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-9-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-9-Version-3.jpg" id="81c7db8e812a9a80205e927c0636a2e9" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/7/77/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-9-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-9-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('81c7db8e812a9a80205e927c0636a2e9')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 9" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/7/77/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-9-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-9-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/77/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-9-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-9-Version-3.jpg" id="81c7db8e812a9a80205e927c0636a2e9" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/7\/77\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-9-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-9-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/7\/77\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-9-Version-3.jpg\/v4-760px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-9-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":760,"bigHeight":570,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num">3</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Nhập văn bản.</b> Bạn gõ văn bản như vẫn làm với các tài liệu khác. Để lưu dòng văn bản vừa gõ và chuyển sang dòng tiếp theo, bạn nhấn <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;"><span class="Unicode">↵</span> Enter</kbd></span>.
<ul><li>Nếu danh mục chứa tệp văn bản mở, bạn chỉ cần nhấp đúp chuột vào tệp văn bản khi nó xuất hiện để thực hiện bước này.</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-19">
<a name="step_2_4" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-10-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 10" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/4/42/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-10-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-10-Version-3.jpg" id="49f176b413543d1b8c503f0acfeeed78" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/4/42/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-10-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-10-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('49f176b413543d1b8c503f0acfeeed78')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 10" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/4/42/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-10-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-10-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/4/42/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-10-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-10-Version-3.jpg" id="49f176b413543d1b8c503f0acfeeed78" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/4\/42\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-10-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-10-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/4\/42\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-10-Version-3.jpg\/v4-760px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-10-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":760,"bigHeight":570,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num">4</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Nhấn <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">Ctrl</kbd>+<kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">Z</kbd></b></span>.</b> Đây là phím lệnh để lưu văn bản và quay về dòng lệnh trong Terminal, cho phép bạn tiếp tục nhập lệnh.<sup id="_ref-1" class="reference" aria-label="Liên kết tới Nguồn 1"><a href="#_note-1">[1]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden id="ts_popup_1" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Nguồn nghiên cứu</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank"></a>

</span></sup>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-110">
<a name="step_2_5" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-11-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 11" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/17/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-11-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-11-Version-3.jpg" id="0fb20ed4c38ebceb52d62b30a1c816cc" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/1/17/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-11-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-11-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('0fb20ed4c38ebceb52d62b30a1c816cc')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 11" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/1/17/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-11-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-11-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/17/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-11-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-11-Version-3.jpg" id="0fb20ed4c38ebceb52d62b30a1c816cc" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/1\/17\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-11-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-11-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/1\/17\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-11-Version-3.jpg\/v4-760px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-11-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":760,"bigHeight":570,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num">5</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Nhập <b><code>ls -l tên tệp.txt</code> vào Terminal.</b></b> Bạn thay "tên tệp" bằng tên định đặt cho tệp văn bản. Câu lệnh này sẽ xác định vị trí tệp để đảm bảo rằng nó đã được tạo trong danh mục bạn chọn.<sup id="_ref-2" class="reference" aria-label="Liên kết tới Nguồn 2"><a href="#_note-2">[2]</a><span class="ts_popup " hidden id="ts_popup_2" style="display: none;">
	<span class="ts_close">X</span>
		<span class="ts_name">Nguồn nghiên cứu</span>
		<span class="ts_description"></span>
				<a href="#" class="ts_source" target="_blank"></a>

</span></sup>
<ul>
<li>Ví dụ: để mở tệp "textfile", bạn nhập lệnh <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">ls -l textfile.txt</kbd>.</li>
<li>Chữ cái trong câu lệnh này là chữ "L" thường, không phải chữ "i" viết hoa.</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-111">
<a name="step_2_6" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-12-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 12" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/6/60/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-12-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-12-Version-3.jpg" id="b07d84a70b612be2663cb333fdba5fb3" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/6/60/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-12-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-12-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('b07d84a70b612be2663cb333fdba5fb3')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 12" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/6/60/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-12-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-12-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/6/60/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-12-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-12-Version-3.jpg" id="b07d84a70b612be2663cb333fdba5fb3" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/6\/60\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-12-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-12-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/6\/60\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-12-Version-3.jpg\/v4-760px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-12-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":760,"bigHeight":570,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num">6</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Nhấn <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;"><span class="Unicode">↵</span> Enter</kbd></b></span>.</b> Đây là thao tác hiển thị thời gian, ngày và tên tệp ở dòng tiếp theo, chỉ ra rằng tệp được tạo và lưu trong danh mục được chọn.
</div>

<div class="section steps  sticky"><div id="cácbước_3" class="section_text">
<h3 class="in-block">
<div class="altblock"><div>Phần <span>3</span><span class="method_of_count"> của 4:</span>
</div>
</div>
<span id="Sử-dụng-Vim"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="S.E1.BB.AD-d.E1.BB.A5ng-Vim">Sử dụng Vim</span>
</h3>
<ol class="steps_list_2">
<li id="step-id-212">
<a name="step_3_1" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-13-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 13" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/b/ba/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-13-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-13-Version-3.jpg" id="805ed1b4622287e11658ff774b1529e1" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/b/ba/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-13-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-13-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('805ed1b4622287e11658ff774b1529e1')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 13" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/b/ba/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-13-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-13-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/b/ba/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-13-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-13-Version-3.jpg" id="805ed1b4622287e11658ff774b1529e1" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/b\/ba\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-13-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-13-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/b\/ba\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-13-Version-3.jpg\/v4-760px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-13-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":760,"bigHeight":570,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num">1</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Nhập <b><code>vi tên tệp.txt</code> vào Terminal.</b></b> Phần "vi" trong câu lệnh này là để chọn sử dụng phần mềm chỉnh sửa văn bản Vim. Bạn sẽ thay "tên tệp" bằng tên tệp văn bản muốn gán với tệp mới.
<ul>
<li>Ví dụ, với tệp "tamins", bạn nhập lệnh <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">vi tamins.txt</kbd>.</li>
<li>Nếu danh mục hiện hành có tệp trùng tên thì lệnh này sẽ mở tệp đó.</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-213">
<a name="step_3_2" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-14-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 14" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/f/fd/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-14-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-14-Version-3.jpg" id="6b8eeac6c1b305d371eb50cff6c0e3d8" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/f/fd/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-14-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-14-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('6b8eeac6c1b305d371eb50cff6c0e3d8')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 14" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/f/fd/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-14-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-14-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/f/fd/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-14-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-14-Version-3.jpg" id="6b8eeac6c1b305d371eb50cff6c0e3d8" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/f\/fd\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-14-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-14-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/f\/fd\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-14-Version-3.jpg\/v4-760px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-14-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":760,"bigHeight":570,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num">2</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Nhấn <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;"><span class="Unicode">↵</span> Enter</kbd></b></span>.</b> Đây là thao tác tạo tệp mới và mở nó trong phần mềm Vim. Bạn sẽ thấy cửa sổ Terminal trống không, có dấu ngã (~) trên mỗi dòng và tên tệp ở phía dưới cửa sổ.
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-214">
<a name="step_3_3" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-15-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 15" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/d/d8/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-15-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-15-Version-3.jpg" id="5316f6a70339d3f46cb81bc85f16a251" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/d/d8/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-15-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-15-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('5316f6a70339d3f46cb81bc85f16a251')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 15" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/d/d8/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-15-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-15-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/d/d8/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-15-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-15-Version-3.jpg" id="5316f6a70339d3f46cb81bc85f16a251" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/d\/d8\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-15-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-15-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/d\/d8\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-15-Version-3.jpg\/v4-760px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-15-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":760,"bigHeight":570,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num">3</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Nhấn phím <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">i</kbd></b></span>.</b> Đây là thao tác đưa tài liệu vào chế độ "Insert" (Chèn) để bạn chỉnh sửa văn bản nếu cần.
<ul><li>Bạn sẽ thấy <b>-- INSERT --</b> xuất hiện ở phía dưới cửa sổ khi nhấn phím <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">I</kbd></span>.</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-215">
<a name="step_3_4" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-16-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 16" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/f/fe/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-16-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-16-Version-3.jpg" id="5e4c7240016bdb717f53aeec2169ec83" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/f/fe/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-16-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-16-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('5e4c7240016bdb717f53aeec2169ec83')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 16" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/f/fe/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-16-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-16-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/f/fe/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-16-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-16-Version-3.jpg" id="5e4c7240016bdb717f53aeec2169ec83" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>

<div class="step_num">4</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Nhập văn bản.</b> Bạn gõ văn bản như vẫn làm với các tài liệu khác. Để lưu dòng văn bản vừa gõ và chuyển sang dòng tiếp theo, chỉ cần nhấn <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;"><span class="Unicode">↵</span> Enter</kbd></span>.
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-216">
<a name="step_3_5" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-17-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 17" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/f/f9/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-17-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-17-Version-3.jpg" id="5c05b2e3deed873e769341f402e4abab" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/f/f9/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-17-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-17-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('5c05b2e3deed873e769341f402e4abab')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 17" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/f/f9/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-17-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-17-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/f/f9/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-17-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-17-Version-3.jpg" id="5c05b2e3deed873e769341f402e4abab" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/f\/f9\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-17-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-17-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/f\/f9\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-17-Version-3.jpg\/v4-760px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-17-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":760,"bigHeight":570,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num">5</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Nhấn phím <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">Esc</kbd></b></span>.</b> Phím này thường nằm ở góc phía trên bên trái bàn phím. Phím này sẽ đưa Vim vào chế độ "Command" (Lệnh).
<ul><li>Bạn sẽ thấy trỏ chuột xuất hiện phía cuối cửa sổ.</li></ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-217">
<a name="step_3_6" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-18-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">

</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 18" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/9/95/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-18-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-18-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/9/95/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-18-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-18-Version-3.jpg" id="14242dbf7ef3ab960f67b827b43e2dde" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/9\/95\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-18-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-18-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/9\/95\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-18-Version-3.jpg\/v4-760px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-18-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":760,"bigHeight":570,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num">6</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Nhập <b><code>:w</code> vào Terminal và nhấn <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;"><span class="Unicode">↵</span> Enter</kbd></b></span>.</b></b> Đây là lệnh lưu tài liệu hiện tại.
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-218">
<a name="step_3_7" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-19-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 19" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/2/21/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-19-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-19-Version-3.jpg" id="fb7b59ea728f6fe35a0b01055938cbf9" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/2/21/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-19-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-19-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('fb7b59ea728f6fe35a0b01055938cbf9')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 19" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/2/21/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-19-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-19-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/2/21/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-19-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-19-Version-3.jpg" id="fb7b59ea728f6fe35a0b01055938cbf9" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/2\/21\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-19-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-19-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/2\/21\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-19-Version-3.jpg\/v4-760px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-19-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":760,"bigHeight":570,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num">7</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Nhập <b><code>:q</code> vào Terminal và nhấn <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;"><span class="Unicode">↵</span> Enter</kbd></b></span>.</b></b> Đây là lệnh thoát Vim và quay trở lại giao diện chính của Terminal. Tệp văn bản hiện nằm trong danh mục được chỉ định.
<ul>
<li>Bạn có thể kiểm tra tệp văn bản bằng cách nhập lệnh <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">ls</kbd> vào Terminal và nhấn <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;"><span class="Unicode">↵</span> Enter</kbd></span>, sau đó tìm tên tệp.</li>
<li>Bạn có thể nhập lệnh <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">:wq</kbd> để lưu và thoát trong cùng 1 lệnh.</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-219">
<a name="step_3_8" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-20-Version-3.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 20" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/10/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-20-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-20-Version-3.jpg" id="afc398f5450ca218908bae5f329cc5f1" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/1/10/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-20-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-20-Version-3.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('afc398f5450ca218908bae5f329cc5f1')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 20" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/1/10/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-20-Version-3.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-20-Version-3.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/10/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-20-Version-3.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-20-Version-3.jpg" id="afc398f5450ca218908bae5f329cc5f1" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/1\/10\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-20-Version-3.jpg\/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-20-Version-3.jpg","bigUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/1\/10\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-20-Version-3.jpg\/v4-760px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-20-Version-3.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":760,"bigHeight":570,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num">8</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Mở lại tệp trong cửa sổ Terminal.</b> Cũng tương tự như tạo tệp, bạn nhập lệnh <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">vi tên tệp.txt</kbd> để mở tệp. Lúc này khi mở tệp, bạn sẽ thấy bất kỳ thay đổi nào mà bạn lưu đều được thực thi.
</div>

<div class="section steps  sticky"><div id="cácbước_4" class="section_text">
<h3 class="in-block">
<div class="altblock"><div>Phần <span>4</span><span class="method_of_count"> của 4:</span>
</div>
</div>
<span id="Sử-dụng-Emacs"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="S.E1.BB.AD-d.E1.BB.A5ng-Emacs">Sử dụng Emacs</span>
</h3>
<ol class="steps_list_2">
<li id="step-id-320">
<a name="step_4_1" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-21.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 21" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/13/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-21.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-21.jpg" id="2b96bfcea5b357be6fe838b1917e6fca" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/1/13/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-21.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-21.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('2b96bfcea5b357be6fe838b1917e6fca')</script>

<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/1\/13\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-21.jpg\/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-21.jpg","bigUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/1\/13\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-21.jpg\/v4-760px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-21.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":760,"bigHeight":570,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num">1</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Nhập <b><code>emacs tên tệp.txt</code> vào Terminal.</b></b> Bạn thay "tên tệp" bằng tên bạn định đặt cho tệp văn bản.
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-321">
<a name="step_4_2" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-22.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 22" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/8/8f/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-22.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-22.jpg" id="ced424301f49e11bb79ab0557d31ad95" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/8/8f/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-22.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-22.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('ced424301f49e11bb79ab0557d31ad95')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 22" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/8/8f/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-22.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-22.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/8/8f/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-22.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-22.jpg" id="ced424301f49e11bb79ab0557d31ad95" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/8\/8f\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-22.jpg\/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-22.jpg","bigUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/8\/8f\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-22.jpg\/v4-760px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-22.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":760,"bigHeight":570,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num">2</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Nhấn <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;"><span class="Unicode">↵</span> Enter</kbd></b></span>.</b> Miễn là tên tệp không bị trùng với tệp văn bản có sẵn trong danh mục hiện hành thì lệnh này sẽ mở tệp văn bản mới trong phần mềm chỉnh sửa Emacs.
<ul>
<li>Ví dụ: tệp tên "newfile" sẽ phải nhập lệnh <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">emacs newfile.txt</kbd>.</li>
<li>Nếu bạn nhập tên tệp đã tồn tại, lệnh này sẽ mở tệp đó.</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-322">
<a name="step_4_3" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-23.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 23" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/4/4c/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-23.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-23.jpg" id="b0ac0a5e086ddb2f7186dcd463641ddb" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/4/4c/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-23.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-23.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('b0ac0a5e086ddb2f7186dcd463641ddb')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 23" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/4/4c/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-23.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-23.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/4/4c/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-23.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-23.jpg" id="b0ac0a5e086ddb2f7186dcd463641ddb" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/4\/4c\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-23.jpg\/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-23.jpg","bigUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/4\/4c\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-23.jpg\/v4-760px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-23.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":760,"bigHeight":570,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num">3</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Tìm hiểu lệnh Emacs.</b> Emacs có vô vàn câu lệnh mạnh mẽ, cho phép điều hướng tài liệu, tra cứu thông tin hỗ trợ hoặc liên quan, điều khiển văn bản và hiểu đoạn mã. Các câu lệnh này được chia làm 2 loại: lệnh Điều khiển và lệnh Meta.
<ul>
<li>
<b>Lệnh Điều khiển</b> có dạng: C-&lt;chữ cái&gt;. Để thực thi lệnh Điều khiển, bạn giữ phím <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">Ctrl</kbd></span> đồng thời nhấn phím chữ cái được chỉ định (ví dụ<span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">Ctrl</kbd></span> và <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">A</kbd></span>).</li>
<li>
<b>Lệnh Meta</b> (hoặc <b>Thoát</b>) có dạng: M-&lt;chữ cái&gt; hoặc ESC &lt;chữ cái&gt;. Chữ "M" ám chỉ phím <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">Alt</kbd></span> hoặc phím <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">Esc</kbd></span> trên máy tính, vì không phải máy tính nào cũng có phím <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">Alt</kbd></span>.</li>
<li>Lệnh được viết như sau <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">C-a b</kbd> (hoặc <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">M-a b</kbd>) yêu cầu bạn nhấn giữ phím <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">Ctrl</kbd></span> (hoặc <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">Alt</kbd></span> hoặc <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">Esc</kbd></span>) đồng thời nhấn phím đầu tiên (ví dụ phím <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">a</kbd></span>), thả cả hai phím rồi ngay lập tức nhấn phím thứ hai (ví dụ phím <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">b</kbd></span>).</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-323">
<a name="step_4_4" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-24.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">

</div>

<div class="step_num">4</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Nhập văn bản.</b> Bạn có thể gõ văn bản như vẫn làm với các tài liệu khác. Để lưu dòng văn bản vừa gõ và chuyển sang dòng tiếp theo, nhấn <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;"><span class="Unicode">↵</span> Enter</kbd></span>.
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-324">
<a name="step_4_5" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-25.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 25" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/f/fc/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-25.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-25.jpg" id="8c16e7e4fa208e2a9ee8df89253b4293" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/f/fc/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-25.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-25.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('8c16e7e4fa208e2a9ee8df89253b4293')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 25" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/f/fc/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-25.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-25.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/f/fc/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-25.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-25.jpg" id="8c16e7e4fa208e2a9ee8df89253b4293" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>

<div class="step_num">5</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Nhấn phím <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">Ctrl</kbd>+<kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">X</kbd></b></span>, rồi nhấn tiếp <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">S</kbd></b></span>.</b> Đây là thao tác lưu tệp.
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</li>
<li id="step-id-325">
<a name="step_4_6" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-26.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 26" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/a/a9/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-26.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-26.jpg" id="a53d94549bef828fc8097842847f986d" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/a/a9/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-26.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-26.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('a53d94549bef828fc8097842847f986d')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 26" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/a/a9/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-26.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-26.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/a/a9/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-26.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-26.jpg" id="a53d94549bef828fc8097842847f986d" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>

<div class="step_num">6</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Nhấn phím <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">Ctrl</kbd>+<kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">X</kbd></b></span>, rồi nhấn tiếp <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><b class="whb"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">Ctrl</kbd>+<kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">C</kbd></b></span>.</b> Đây là thao tác thoát phần mềm chỉnh sửa Emacs và quay trở về danh mục trong Terminal. Tệp văn bản được lưu dưới tên bạn vừa đặt trong danh mục này.
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</li>
<li class="final_li" id="step-id-326">
<a name="step_4_7" class="stepanchor"></a><div class="mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter " style="max-width:728px"><a href="#/T%E1%BA%ADp_tin:Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-27.jpg" class="image"><div class="content-spacer">
<img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 27" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/d/d5/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-27.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-27.jpg" id="fcc5e580a51ce4f5b152a0626065de23" data-width="460" data-height="345" data-src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/d/d5/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-27.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-27.jpg"><script>WH.shared.addScrollLoadItem('fcc5e580a51ce4f5b152a0626065de23')</script>
</div>
<noscript><img alt="Tiêu đề ảnh Create and Edit Text File in Linux by Using Terminal Step 27" src="https://www.wikihow.com/images_en/thumb/d/d5/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-27.jpg/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-27.jpg" decoding="async" class="whcdn content-fill" data-srclarge="https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/d/d5/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-27.jpg/v4-728px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-27.jpg" id="fcc5e580a51ce4f5b152a0626065de23" data-width="460" data-height="345"></noscript>
<div class="image_details" style="display:none;"><span style="display:none;">{"smallUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/d\/d5\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-27.jpg\/v4-460px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-27.jpg","bigUrl":"https:\/\/www.wikihow.com\/images_en\/thumb\/d\/d5\/Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-27.jpg\/v4-760px-Create-and-Edit-Text-File-in-Linux-by-Using-Terminal-Step-27.jpg","smallWidth":460,"smallHeight":345,"bigWidth":760,"bigHeight":570,"licensing":"&lt;div class=\"mw-parser-output\"&gt;&lt;\/div&gt;"}</span></div></a></div>
<div class="step_num">7</div><div class="step">
<b class="whb">Mở lại tệp văn bản.</b> Để mở tệp, bạn nhập lệnh <kbd style="background:#EEEEEE; letter-spacing:0.1em; padding-left:0.5em; padding-right:0.4em;">emacs tên tệp.txt</kbd> vào Terminal. Miễn là bạn ở trong danh mục chứa tệp thì lệnh này có thể mở tệp trong Emacs, vậy là bạn có thể tiếp tục chỉnh sửa nếu muốn.
</div>
<div class="clearall"></div>
<div class="wh_ad_inner" data-service="adsense" data-slot="6771527778" data-width="728" data-height="90" data-smallheight="250" data-type="method" data-small="1" data-medium="1" data-channels="8567383174,4819709854,3614436449" data-mobilechannels="8567383174" data-observerloading="1">
<div id="mobilemethod_ad_4"></div>
<div class="ad_label_method">Quảng cáo</div>
</div>
<script>WH.ads.addBodyAd('mobilemethod_ad_4')</script>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</div></div>
</div>
<div class="section lờikhuyên sticky">
<h2 class="section-heading" onclick="javascript:mfTempOpenSection(2)">
<div class="mw-ui-icon mw-ui-icon-element indicator"></div>
<span id="Lời-khuyên"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="L.E1.BB.9Di-khuy.C3.AAn">Lời khuyên</span>
</h2>
<div id="lờikhuyên" class="section_text">
<ul>
<li>Bạn có thể truy cập Vim trên bất kỳ phiên bản nào của Linux, trong khi phần mềm Emacs lại chi tiết hơn giúp người mới dễ sử dụng.</li>
<li>Bạn có thể mở màn hình "Trợ giúp" của Emacs bằng cách nhấn đồng thời <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">Ctrl</kbd>+<kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">H</kbd></span>, sau đó thả cả hai phím rồi nhấn tiếp phím <span style="white-space: nowrap;"><kbd class="keyboard-key nowrap" style="border: 3px outset #F3F3F3; border-left-color: #DBDBDB; border-top-color: #DBDBDB; background-color: #F3F3F3; padding: 0px 2px; font-family: inherit; font-size: 0.85em;">T</kbd></span>. Trình đơn Trợ giúp sẽ hiển thị nhiều lệnh bổ sung và các chức năng khác trong phần mềm Emacs, có thể sẽ có ích cho bạn trong quá trình nhập văn bản.</li>
</ul>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="mf-section-2 collapsible-block" id="mf-section-2">
</div>
<div class="section cảnhbáo sticky">
<h2 class="section-heading" onclick="javascript:mfTempOpenSection(3)">
<div class="mw-ui-icon mw-ui-icon-element indicator"></div>
<span id="Cảnh-báo"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="C.E1.BA.A3nh-b.C3.A1o">Cảnh báo</span>
</h2>
<div id="cảnhbáo" class="section_text">
<ul><li>Có thể sẽ không có cảnh báo nếu bạn quên không lưu tài liệu trước khi đóng, đặc biệt là trong phần mềm Vim. Luôn nhớ lưu tài liệu trước khi đóng.</li></ul>
<div class="clearall"></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="mf-section-3 collapsible-block" id="mf-section-3">

	<h2 id="sp_h2"><span class="mw-headline">Về bài wikiHow này</span></h2>

	<div id="social_proof_mobile">
		<a name="social_proof_anchor" id="social_proof_anchor"></a>
		<div class="sp_inner">
				<div class="sp_top_box sp_person sp_staff">
					<div class="sp_top_icon_bg">
						<div class="sp_top_icon_check"></div>
						<div class="sp_staff_icon"></div>
					</div>
					<div class="sp_expert_text sp_top_box_hoverable sp_nonverifier_text">
						<div>
							<div id="sp_expert_team_label">Đồng tác giả:</div>
							<div id="sp_expert_team">Biên tập viên wikiHow</div>
							<div id="sp_expert_blurb"></div>
						</div>
					</div>
				</div>
			<div id="sp_expert_desc">
			Bài viết này có đồng tác giả là đội ngũ biên tập viên và các nhà nghiên cứu đã qua đào tạo, những người xác nhận tính chính xác và toàn diện của bài viết. 
			</div>
